msg:1. The location is very good. On the main street of Wuyishan, you can find delicious food at both ends. It is also very close to the bus station, so it is very convenient to go out.
2. The design is beautiful. The design is really amazing, worthy of being an award-winning work, with a sense of bamboo rhyme and tea fragrance. The first and second floors can be connected through the inner courtyard, which is seamless.
3. Complete facilities. There is a special space for tea tasting indoors, with complete tea sets and good tea. The only drawback is that there is only a washing machine but no dryer, which is too difficult in this humid and rainy place. It feels damp every day.
4. Breakfast. The breakfast is delicious, with rice noodles and Dahongpao tea eggs, which can meet the needs of breakfast.

msg:The hotel is very close to the south entrance of Wuyi Mountain and the tram. If you take the high-speed rail to Nanping, you can take the tram for 40 minutes to the south entrance, and then take a taxi for more than ten yuan to the hotel. It is very convenient to eat around. There are many restaurants to choose from within a 10-minute walk, and takeout can be delivered directly to the room. The guest room is generally clean, and the staff service is good, but there are not many sockets in the room, and there is no desk. If you bring a computer to work, the computer can only be placed on the bed. In addition, only two bottles of water are provided free of charge every day, and more are charged. This is the first time I have encountered this when staying in a hotel.

posted:Posted April 23, 2024
msg:The location of the hotel is very good. There is a free bus that goes directly to the scenic spot, the light rail station and the Impression Dahongpao at the door. You don't need to take a taxi for a few days. The restaurant next to it is also delicious, and the tea shop is also good. I bought a lot of tea. The facilities are basically good, with Chinese decoration. The rooms were full for the first two days, so I didn't get an upgrade. The basic room is not very good. 32 square meters sounds not small, but the toilet is bigger than the room. After opening the window, there is a rumble of three air-conditioning units. Fortunately, I got an upgrade for the next two nights, otherwise it would be really frustrating. The breakfast is also better than expected. The waiters are very enthusiastic and take the initiative to say hello. There are two small points. The first is that the room has to be charged for water delivery. It's the first time I've stayed in a hotel that charges for ordinary bottled water. It's so strange. It is recommended to make this clear when checking in. The second is that there is only a washing machine but no dryer. The clothes can't be dried at all after being cold for a day and a night. It is recommended to install it. Overall good~

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Guestroom (Double bed)
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted July 16, 2021
msg:"A stream runs through the mountains, with nine curves of clear water. There are rocks beside the stream, and the reflection is soaked in cold green."

The beautiful scenery of Wuyi is as unforgettable as described in poetry, and this hotel undoubtedly perfectly reflects the charm of this place. The gray square shape like the huge rock unique to Wuyi Mountain is particularly conspicuous on this street. The unique design style directly clashes with the Wuyi landscape, but is not obtrusive. Entering the hotel lobby is a familiar scent, and the quiet and melodious music brings a touch of Zen. The entire hotel implements the elements of tea. In addition to some rare tea-related exhibits, there is also a public tea-making area, which is quite like a tea museum.

It is said that the road design of the hotel is as winding as a Jiuqu River, and the connections between buildings are structured by countless elevators. Next to these roads are ornamental courtyards carefully designed by designers. The tranquility and elegance are the first impression they gave me. The collision of gray stones and towering pine trees has a wabi-sabi style flavor. Every corner is a scene, and it contains the designerâ€™s intentions. It is undoubtedly a good place for taking pictures.

People, people in Wuyi Mountain have always given me a feeling of seeing things clearly, at least the tea farmers I met are like this. But all the enthusiasm I received in Wuyishan was given by the hotel's service staff. They are patient, gentle, and willing to solve problems. You seem to be able to see the unique charm conveyed by tea from them. Especially the lady named Zhang at the front desk, I personally think that Narcissus is synonymous with her, soft and gentle. She took the trouble to solve many of my problems, and the foundation of my happiness on this trip came from her help.

Turning back to the hotel itself, there are still many things to be desired. First of all, the design of the sink is unreasonable (for me) and it is very easy to splash water. The mouthwash cup does not feel very good when used, and it is a bit contrary to ergonomics. Secondly, I booked a suite worth thousands of dollars, but the walls were cracked and not repaired, which somewhat affected my mood. Finally, although the breakfast selection is very rich, more changes can be added every day to cater for travelers who need to stay for a long time. btw Friends who choose room types should check in advance whether the construction on the outside of the suite has been completed in the near future, otherwise you will wake up at 7 or 8 in the morning with the sound of banging, and enjoy the forest formed by the construction green cloth outside the window.
----------------------------------------
